gnt_em_vb__te\" aria-label=\"Fears are mounting around the world following the assassination of Iranian&nbsp;General Qasem Soleimani&nbsp;- but is&nbsp;World War 3&nbsp;about to happen?\" data-c-credit=\"Just the FAQs, USA TODAY\"></div></aside><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">Americans should be on heightened alert for cyberattacks after <a href=\"https://www.usatoday.com/story/news/world/2020/01/07/iran-state-tv-tehran-fires-iraqi-base-housing-us-troops-ain-assad/2837693001/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-t-l=\"|inline|intext|n/a\" class=\"gnt_ar_b_a\">Iran fired more than a dozen missiles</a>&nbsp;at two&nbsp;military bases in Iraq where U.S. troops are stationed late Tuesday.</p><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">The FBI said Wednesday that the&nbsp;bureau is \u201caware of the continued possibility that retaliatory actions could be taken against the United States and its interests abroad.\u201d</p><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">\u201cWhile there is no specific or credible threat to the homeland at this time, we urge the public to be vigilant and report any suspicious activity to law enforcement,\u201d the FBI said.</p><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">On Monday Homeland Security <a href=\"https://www.us-cert.gov/ncas/alerts/aa20-006a\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-t-l=\"|inline|intext|n/a\" class=\"gnt_ar_b_a\">urged cybersecurity teams</a> to \"enhance monitoring of network and email traffic,\" including for email phishing attempts.</p><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">Iran, which has been linked to&nbsp;cyber attacks against Saudi Arabia and&nbsp;the Sands Las Vegas casino owned by Sheldon Adelson, could target private businesses and government infrastructure to avenge last week's&nbsp;killing of its top military commander as tensions between Tehran and Washington <a href=\"https://www.usatoday.com/story/news/politics/2020/01/06/iran-tension-soleimani-explainer/2822590001/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-t-l=\"|inline|intext|n/a\" class=\"gnt_ar_b_a\">reach one of their highest points</a> since the 1979 Iranian revolution, security researchers say.</p><aside aria-label=\"advertisement\" class=\"gnt_m gnt_x gnt_x__lbl gnt_x__al\"><div data-g-r=\"lazy\" data-gl-method=\"lazyLoadX\" id=\"~ad-slot-7103-usatoday-native-article_link-tech-2\" class=\"gnt_x_sl gnt_x_al\"></div></aside><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">In&nbsp;retaliation for the U.S. drone strike that killed Qasem Soleimani in Baghdad, Iran could go after the power and electricity you use, the smart devices you carry or&nbsp;your bank account, they say.&nbsp;</p><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">\"As these escalations continue to play out and definitely in wake of Soleimani's death, America needs to be prepared&nbsp;for retaliation,\" said Graham Brookie, director of the Atlantic Council's Digital Forensic Research Lab. \"Are we being attacked online? No, not that we can prove and not that is having an impact that is blatant or at scale or moving the needle on public conversation or crippling any infrastructure.\"</p><aside class=\"gnt_em TODAY\"></div></aside><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\"><strong class=\"gnt_ar_b_al\">Cyberwar with Iran:</strong><a href=\"https://www.usatoday.com/story/tech/2020/01/03/how-much-damage-could-iran-cyber-attacks-do/2803599001/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-t-l=\"|inline|intext|n/a\" class=\"gnt_ar_b_a\">How vulnerable is America?</a></p><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">A cyber conflict has been <a href=\"https://www.usatoday.com/story/tech/2020/01/03/how-much-damage-could-iran-cyber-attacks-do/2803599001/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-t-l=\"|inline|intext|n/a\" class=\"gnt_ar_b_a\">silently raging for years</a>.<strong>&nbsp;</strong>Even if no attack from Iran occurs in coming weeks, \"the&nbsp;danger zone will extend for years,\"&nbsp;warned Steven Bellovin, a computer science professor at Columbia University School of Engineering.&nbsp;</p><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">For nearly a decade, Iran has been building up its cyber arsenal and is now considered among the&nbsp;major&nbsp;nation-state threats to the security of&nbsp;the U.S.</p><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">\"The Iranian regime has demonstrated greater appetite towards destructive or disruptive cyber-attacks in peacetime than any other nation,\" <a href=\"https://www.f-secure.com/en/consulting/our-thinking/understanding-the-cyber-threat-from-iran\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-t-l=\"|inline|intext|n/a\" class=\"gnt_ar_b_a\">say</a> Ed Parsons and George Michael, who research cyber threats to the private sector.</p><figure class=\"gnt_em gnt_em_img\"><img class=\"gnt_em_img_i\" style=\"height:440px\" data-g-r=\"lazy\" 2020.\" data-c-credit=\"Erfan Kouchari, AP\"></div></figure><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">Secretary of State Mike Pompeo acknowledged last week that Iran could unleash cyberattacks.</p><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">\u201cThe Iranians have a deep and complex cyber capability, to be sure,\u201d Pompeo said on Fox News. \u201cKnow that we have certainly considered that risk.\"</p><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">On Saturday, the Department of Homeland Security <a href=\"https://www.dhs.gov/sites/default/files/ntas/alerts/20_0104_ntas_bulletin.pdf\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-t-l=\"|inline|intext|n/a\" class=\"gnt_ar_b_a\">warned</a> Americans that Iran is capable of launching cyberattacks with \u201ctemporary disruptive effects\u201d against critical U.S. infrastructure, though it had \u201cno information indicating a specific, credible threat to the Homeland.\u201d&nbsp;</p><aside aria-label=\"advertisement\" class=\"gnt_m gnt_x gnt_x__lbl gnt_x__al\"><div data-g-r=\"lazy\" data-gl-method=\"lazyLoadX\" id=\"~ad-slot-7103-usatoday-native-article_link-tech-3\" class=\"gnt_x_sl gnt_x_al\"></div></aside><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\"><strong class=\"gnt_ar_b_al\">'This was an act of war':</strong><a href=\"https://www.usatoday.com/story/news/politics/2020/01/07/iran-missile-strikes-us-bases-reaction/2838233001/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-t-l=\"|inline|intext|n/a\" class=\"gnt_ar_b_a\">Lawmakers react to Iran's missile strike on US military bases</a></p><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">The National Terrorism System advisory recommended that Americans take precautions by backing up data and using two-factor authentication for sensitive accounts.</p><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">Acting Homeland Security Secretary Chad Wolf <a href=\"https://twitter.com/DHS_Wolf/status/1213585937881534467\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-t-l=\"|inline|intext|n/a\" class=\"gnt_ar_b_a\">tweeted</a> that the bulletin was intended to \u201cinform &amp; reassure the American public, state/local governments &amp; private partners that DHS is actively monitoring &amp; preparing for any specific, credible threat, should one arise.\u201d</p><aside class=\"gnt_em gnt_em_anc\" id=\"gnt_atomsnc\" data-g-r=\"lazy\" data-gl-method=\"loadAnc\" aria-label=\"Newsletter signup form\"></aside><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">On Sunday, a&nbsp;federal website went&nbsp;offline after a <a href=\"https://www.usatoday.com/story/news/nation/2020/01/05/iran-hack-homeland-security-website-hacked-image-bloody-trump/2818308001/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-t-l=\"|inline|intext|n/a\" class=\"gnt_ar_b_a\">hacker uploaded photos to the site that included an Iranian flag and an image depicting a bloodied President Donald Trump</a> being punched in the face.</p><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">The images appeared on the Federal Depository Library Program program's website late Saturday before the site was taken offline. The Cybersecurity and Infrastructure Security Agency, a division of the Department of Homeland Security, said it was monitoring the situation.</p><figure class=\"gnt_em gnt_em_img\"><img class=\"gnt_em_img_i\" style=\"height:372px\" data-g-r=\"lazy\" data-gl-src=\"https://www.gannett-cdn.com/-mm-/21dd4538ee6338cfe86b3cec0e65f5b54cac1573/c=0-128-2095-1306/local/-/media/2019/12/24/USATODAY/usatsports/hacker-in-hoodie-identity-theft-cyber-security.jpg?width=660&amp;height=372&amp;fit=crop&amp;format=pjpg&amp;auto=webp\" data-gl-srcset=\"https://www.gannett-cdn.com/-mm-/21dd4538ee6338cfe86b3cec0e65f5b54cac1573/c=0-128-2095-1306/local/-/media/2019/12/24/USATODAY/usatsports/hacker-in-hoodie-identity-theft-cyber-security.jpg?width=1320&amp;height=744&amp;fit=crop&amp;format=pjpg&amp;auto=webp 2x\" decoding=\"async\" alt=\"Someone in a hooded sweatshirt with their face obscured, illustrating cybercrime.\"><div class=\"gnt_em_img_ccw gnt_em_img_ccw__cap gnt_em_img_ccw__crd\" data-c-caption=\"Someone in a hooded sweatshirt with their face obscured, illustrating cybercrime.\" data-c-credit=\"Getty Images\"></div></figure><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">\"We are aware the website of the Federal Depository Library Program was defaced with pro-Iranian, anti-US messaging,\" the cybersecurity agency said in a statement. \"At this time, there is no confirmation that this was the action of Iranian state-sponsored actors. The website was taken offline and is no longer accessible.\"</p><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">The statement added that \"in these times of increased threats\" all organizations should increase cyber monitoring, back up IT systems, implement secure authentication and have an incident response plan ready should a hack take place.</p><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">CrowdStrike, a cybersecurity firm that warned of increasing cyberattacks by Iran earlier this year, said Monday that industries such as oil and gas and electricity could be targets.</p><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">\u201cCrowdStrike Intelligence believes that Iranian adversaries are likely to leverage a broad range of means, including cyber operations, against U.S. and allied interests,\u201d the company said. \u201cOur current assessment is that organizations in the financial, defense, government, and oil and gas sectors are the most likely targets for retaliation activity.\u201d</p><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\"><strong class=\"gnt_ar_b_al\">What we know:</strong><a href=\"https://www.usatoday.com/story/news/politics/2020/01/07/u-s-military-bases-attacked-iranian-missiles-what-we-know/2838092001/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-t-l=\"|inline|intext|n/a\" class=\"gnt_ar_b_a\">US military bases attacked by Iran have hosted Trump and Pence, damage unclear</a></p><a class=\"gnt_em gnt_em_gl gnt_em__el\" href=\"/picture-gallery/money/2020/01/08/financial-markets-around-world-react-iran-missile-strike/2841486001/\" data-t-l=\"|inlinePhotoGalleryPromo|viewGallery\" aria-label=\"View Gallery - Financial markets around the world react to Iran missile strike\" data-g-r=\"nav_mo\" data-g-tn=\"pgcss\" data-g-mtn=\"pg2841486001\" data-g-moh=\"hpgm\" aria-haspopup=\"dialog\" aria-expanded=\"false\" data-c-id=\"2841486001\"><img class=\"gnt_em_gl_i\" data-g-r=\"lazy\" data-gl-src=\"https://www.gannett-cdn.com/presto/2020/01/08/USAT/9fd3b55c-10f4-4dd2-b494-be76f8a199e0-22821.jpg?crop=3999,2249,x1,y411&amp;width=660&amp;height=372&amp;format=pjpg&amp;auto=webp\" data-gl-srcset=\"https://www.gannett-cdn.com/presto/2020/01/08/USAT/9fd3b55c-10f4-4dd2-b494-be76f8a199e0-22821.jpg?crop=3999,2249,x1,y411&amp;width=1320&amp;height=744&amp;format=pjpg&amp;auto=webp 2x\" decoding=\"async\" alt=\"\"><div class=\"gnt_em_gl_i_nt\"></div><div class=\"gnt_em_gl_vg\" data-c-tc=\"5\"><svg class=\"gnt_em_gl_vg_svg__ca\"><use xlink:href=\"#gnt_svg_camera\"></use></svg><svg class=\"gnt_em_gl_vg_svg\"><use xlink:href=\"#gnt_svg_expand\"></use></svg></div><div class=\"gnt_em_t gnt_em_t__hb\" data-c-et=\"Financial markets around the world react to Iran missile strike\" aria-label=\"Oil prices rose and Asian stock markets fell Wednesday after Iran fired missiles at U.S. bases in Iraq.\"></div></a><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">CrowdStrike said it was monitoring for denial of service and ransomware attacks, tools frequently deployed by Iranian hackers.</p><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">Iran intensified its cyber warfare capabilities after&nbsp;the&nbsp;Stuxnet&nbsp;computer worm, a&nbsp;program believed to have been run by the United States and Israel, was uncovered. The worm destroyed nuclear centrifuges at the Natanz uranium enrichment plant.</p><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">\u201cStuxnet caused Iran to really wake up: 'Hey this cyber stuff is really powerful. We can do this, too.' And unlike nuclear weapons, it doesn\u2019t take a huge industrial infrastructure,\" Bellovin said.</p><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">\"Iran\u2019s abilities have gotten noticeably stronger over the last 10 years,\" with&nbsp;hackers targeting&nbsp;major U.S. financial institutions, universities and companies, he said.</p><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">Bellovin warns that&nbsp;it could take years for Iran to launch a cyberattack. American companies should shore up their defenses accordingly, he said.</p><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\">\"I worry about companies letting down their guard,\" Bellovin&nbsp;said. \"If people get an alert and then after three weeks revert to business as usual, two years from now they may find themselves hit badly.\"</p><p class=\"gnt_ar_b_p\"><em>Contributing: Kevin Johnson</em></p></div><div
